</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L4" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="4"></td>
        <td id="LC4" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Clients of memcached communicate with server through TCP connections.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L5" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="5"></td>
        <td id="LC5" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(A UDP interface is also available; details are below under &quot;UDP</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L6" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="6"></td>
        <td id="LC6" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">protocol.&quot;) A given running memcached server listens on some</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L7" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="7"></td>
        <td id="LC7" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(configurable) port; clients connect to that port, send commands to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L8" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="8"></td>
        <td id="LC8" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the server, read responses, and eventually close the connection.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L9" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="9"></td>
        <td id="LC9" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L10" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="10"></td>
        <td id="LC10" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">There is no need to send any command to end the session. A client may</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L11" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="11"></td>
        <td id="LC11" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">just close the connection at any moment it no longer needs it. Note,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L12" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="12"></td>
        <td id="LC12" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">however, that clients are encouraged to cache their connections rather</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L13" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="13"></td>
        <td id="LC13" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">than reopen them every time they need to store or retrieve data.  This</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L14" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="14"></td>
        <td id="LC14" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">is because memcached is especially designed to work very efficiently</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L15" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="15"></td>
        <td id="LC15" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">with a very large number (many hundreds, more than a thousand if</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L16" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="16"></td>
        <td id="LC16" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">necessary) of open connections. Caching connections will eliminate the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L17" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="17"></td>
        <td id="LC17" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">overhead associated with establishing a TCP connection (the overhead</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L18" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="18"></td>
        <td id="LC18" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">of preparing for a new connection on the server side is insignificant</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L19" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="19"></td>
        <td id="LC19" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">compared to this).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L20" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="20"></td>
        <td id="LC20" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L21" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="21"></td>
        <td id="LC21" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">There are two kinds of data sent in the memcache protocol: text lines</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L22" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="22"></td>
        <td id="LC22" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and unstructured data.  Text lines are used for commands from clients</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L23" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="23"></td>
        <td id="LC23" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and responses from servers. Unstructured data is sent when a client</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L24" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="24"></td>
        <td id="LC24" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">wants to store or retrieve data. The server will transmit back</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L25" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="25"></td>
        <td id="LC25" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">unstructured data in exactly the same way it received it, as a byte</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L26" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="26"></td>
        <td id="LC26" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">stream. The server doesn&#39;t care about byte order issues in</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L27" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="27"></td>
        <td id="LC27" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">unstructured data and isn&#39;t aware of them. There are no limitations on</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L28" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="28"></td>
        <td id="LC28" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">characters that may appear in unstructured data; however, the reader</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L29" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="29"></td>
        <td id="LC29" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">of such data (either a client or a server) will always know, from a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L30" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="30"></td>
        <td id="LC30" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">preceding text line, the exact length of the data block being</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L31" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="31"></td>
        <td id="LC31" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">transmitted.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L32" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="32"></td>
        <td id="LC32" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L33" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="33"></td>
        <td id="LC33" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Text lines are always terminated by \r\n. Unstructured data is _also_</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L34" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="34"></td>
        <td id="LC34" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">terminated by \r\n, even though \r, \n or any other 8-bit characters</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L35" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="35"></td>
        <td id="LC35" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">may also appear inside the data. Therefore, when a client retrieves</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L36" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="36"></td>
        <td id="LC36" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">data from a server, it must use the length of the data block (which it</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L37" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="37"></td>
        <td id="LC37" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">will be provided with) to determine where the data block ends, and not</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L38" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="38"></td>
        <td id="LC38" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the fact that \r\n follows the end of the data block, even though it</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L39" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="39"></td>
        <td id="LC39" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">does.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L40" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="40"></td>
        <td id="LC40" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L41" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="41"></td>
        <td id="LC41" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Keys</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L42" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="42"></td>
        <td id="LC42" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">----</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L43" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="43"></td>
        <td id="LC43" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L44" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="44"></td>
        <td id="LC44" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Data stored by memcached is identified with the help of a key. A key</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L45" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="45"></td>
        <td id="LC45" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">is a text string which should uniquely identify the data for clients</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L46" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="46"></td>
        <td id="LC46" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">that are interested in storing and retrieving it.  Currently the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L47" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="47"></td>
        <td id="LC47" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">length limit of a key is set at 250 characters (of course, normally</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L48" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="48"></td>
        <td id="LC48" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">clients wouldn&#39;t need to use such long keys); the key must not include</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L49" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="49"></td>
        <td id="LC49" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">control characters or whitespace.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L50" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="50"></td>
        <td id="LC50" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L51" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="51"></td>
        <td id="LC51" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Commands</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L52" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="52"></td>
        <td id="LC52" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">--------</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L53" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="53"></td>
        <td id="LC53" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L54" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="54"></td>
        <td id="LC54" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">There are three types of commands.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L55" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="55"></td>
        <td id="LC55" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L56" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="56"></td>
        <td id="LC56" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Storage commands (there are six: &quot;set&quot;, &quot;add&quot;, &quot;replace&quot;, &quot;append&quot;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L57" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="57"></td>
        <td id="LC57" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">&quot;prepend&quot; and &quot;cas&quot;) ask the server to store some data identified by a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L58" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="58"></td>
        <td id="LC58" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">key. The client sends a command line, and then a data block; after</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L59" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="59"></td>
        <td id="LC59" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">that the client expects one line of response, which will indicate</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L60" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="60"></td>
        <td id="LC60" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">success or failure.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L61" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="61"></td>
        <td id="LC61" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L62" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="62"></td>
        <td id="LC62" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Retrieval commands (there are two: &quot;get&quot; and &quot;gets&quot;) ask the server to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L63" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="63"></td>
        <td id="LC63" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">retrieve data corresponding to a set of keys (one or more keys in one</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L64" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="64"></td>
        <td id="LC64" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">request). The client sends a command line, which includes all the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L65" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="65"></td>
        <td id="LC65" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">requested keys; after that for each item the server finds it sends to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L66" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="66"></td>
        <td id="LC66" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the client one response line with information about the item, and one</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L67" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="67"></td>
        <td id="LC67" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">data block with the item&#39;s data; this continues until the server</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L68" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="68"></td>
        <td id="LC68" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">finished with the &quot;END&quot; response line.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L69" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="69"></td>
        <td id="LC69" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L70" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="70"></td>
        <td id="LC70" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">All other commands don&#39;t involve unstructured data. In all of them,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L71" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="71"></td>
        <td id="LC71" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the client sends one command line, and expects (depending on the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L72" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="72"></td>
        <td id="LC72" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">command) either one line of response, or several lines of response</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L73" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="73"></td>
        <td id="LC73" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">ending with &quot;END&quot; on the last line.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L74" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="74"></td>
        <td id="LC74" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L75" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="75"></td>
        <td id="LC75" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A command line always starts with the name of the command, followed by</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L76" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="76"></td>
        <td id="LC76" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">parameters (if any) delimited by whitespace. Command names are</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L77" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="77"></td>
        <td id="LC77" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">lower-case and are case-sensitive.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L78" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="78"></td>
        <td id="LC78" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L79" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="79"></td>
        <td id="LC79" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Expiration times</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L80" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="80"></td>
        <td id="LC80" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">----------------</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L81" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="81"></td>
        <td id="LC81" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L82" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="82"></td>
        <td id="LC82" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Some commands involve a client sending some kind of expiration time</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L83" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="83"></td>
        <td id="LC83" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(relative to an item or to an operation requested by the client) to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L84" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="84"></td>
        <td id="LC84" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the server. In all such cases, the actual value sent may either be</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L85" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="85"></td>
        <td id="LC85" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Unix time (number of seconds since January 1, 1970, as a 32-bit</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L86" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="86"></td>
        <td id="LC86" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">value), or a number of seconds starting from current time. In the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L87" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="87"></td>
        <td id="LC87" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">latter case, this number of seconds may not exceed 60*60*24*30 (number</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L88" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="88"></td>
        <td id="LC88" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">of seconds in 30 days); if the number sent by a client is larger than</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L89" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="89"></td>
        <td id="LC89" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">that, the server will consider it to be real Unix time value rather</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L90" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="90"></td>
        <td id="LC90" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">than an offset from current time.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L91" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="91"></td>
        <td id="LC91" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L92" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="92"></td>
        <td id="LC92" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L93" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="93"></td>
        <td id="LC93" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Error strings</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L94" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="94"></td>
        <td id="LC94" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">-------------</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L95" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="95"></td>
        <td id="LC95" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L96" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="96"></td>
        <td id="LC96" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Each command sent by a client may be answered with an error string</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L97" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="97"></td>
        <td id="LC97" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">from the server. These error strings come in three types:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L98" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="98"></td>
        <td id="LC98" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L99" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="99"></td>
        <td id="LC99" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &quot;ERROR\r\n&quot;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L100" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="100"></td>
        <td id="LC100" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L101" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="101"></td>
        <td id="LC101" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  means the client sent a nonexistent command name.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L102" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="102"></td>
        <td id="LC102" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L103" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="103"></td>
        <td id="LC103" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &quot;CLIENT_ERROR &lt;error&gt;\r\n&quot;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L104" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="104"></td>
        <td id="LC104" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L105" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="105"></td>
        <td id="LC105" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  means some sort of client error in the input line, i.e. the input</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L106" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="106"></td>
        <td id="LC106" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  doesn&#39;t conform to the protocol in some way. &lt;error&gt; is a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L107" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="107"></td>
        <td id="LC107" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  human-readable error string.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L108" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="108"></td>
        <td id="LC108" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L109" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="109"></td>
        <td id="LC109" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &quot;SERVER_ERROR &lt;error&gt;\r\n&quot;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L110" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="110"></td>
        <td id="LC110" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L111" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="111"></td>
        <td id="LC111" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  means some sort of server error prevents the server from carrying</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L112" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="112"></td>
        <td id="LC112" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  out the command. &lt;error&gt; is a human-readable error string. In cases</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L113" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="113"></td>
        <td id="LC113" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  of severe server errors, which make it impossible to continue</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L114" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="114"></td>
        <td id="LC114" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  serving the client (this shouldn&#39;t normally happen), the server will</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L115" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="115"></td>
        <td id="LC115" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  close the connection after sending the error line. This is the only</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L116" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="116"></td>
        <td id="LC116" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  case in which the server closes a connection to a client.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L117" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="117"></td>
        <td id="LC117" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L118" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="118"></td>
        <td id="LC118" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L119" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="119"></td>
        <td id="LC119" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In the descriptions of individual commands below, these error lines</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L120" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="120"></td>
        <td id="LC120" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">are not again specifically mentioned, but clients must allow for their</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L121" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="121"></td>
        <td id="LC121" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">possibility.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L122" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="122"></td>
        <td id="LC122" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L123" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="123"></td>
        <td id="LC123" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L124" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="124"></td>
        <td id="LC124" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Storage commands</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L125" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="125"></td>
        <td id="LC125" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">----------------</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L126" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="126"></td>
        <td id="LC126" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L127" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="127"></td>
        <td id="LC127" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">First, the client sends a command line which looks like this:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L128" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="128"></td>
        <td id="LC128" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L129" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="129"></td>
        <td id="LC129" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">&lt;command name&gt; &lt;key&gt; &lt;flags&gt; &lt;exptime&gt; &lt;bytes&gt; [noreply]\r\n</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L130" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="130"></td>
        <td id="LC130" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">cas &lt;key&gt; &lt;flags&gt; &lt;exptime&gt; &lt;bytes&gt; &lt;cas unique&gt; [noreply]\r\n</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L131" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="131"></td>
        <td id="LC131" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L132" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="132"></td>
        <td id="LC132" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &lt;command name&gt; is &quot;set&quot;, &quot;add&quot;, &quot;replace&quot;, &quot;append&quot; or &quot;prepend&quot;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L133" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="133"></td>
        <td id="LC133" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L134" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="134"></td>
        <td id="LC134" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  &quot;set&quot; means &quot;store this data&quot;.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L135" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="135"></td>
        <td id="LC135" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L136" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="136"></td>
        <td id="LC136" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  &quot;add&quot; means &quot;store this data, but only if the server *doesn&#39;t* already</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L137" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="137"></td>
        <td id="LC137" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  hold data for this key&quot;.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L138" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="138"></td>
        <td id="LC138" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L139" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="139"></td>
        <td id="LC139" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  &quot;replace&quot; means &quot;store this data, but only if the server *does*</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L140" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="140"></td>
        <td id="LC140" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  already hold data for this key&quot;.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L141" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="141"></td>
        <td id="LC141" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L142" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="142"></td>
        <td id="LC142" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  &quot;append&quot; means &quot;add this data to an existing key after existing data&quot;.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L143" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="143"></td>
        <td id="LC143" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L144" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="144"></td>
        <td id="LC144" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  &quot;prepend&quot; means &quot;add this data to an existing key before existing data&quot;.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L145" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="145"></td>
        <td id="LC145" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L146" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="146"></td>
        <td id="LC146" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The append and prepend commands do not accept flags or exptime.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L147" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="147"></td>
        <td id="LC147" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  They update existing data portions, and ignore new flag and exptime</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L148" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="148"></td>
        <td id="LC148" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  settings.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L149" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="149"></td>
        <td id="LC149" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L150" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="150"></td>
        <td id="LC150" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  &quot;cas&quot; is a check and set operation which means &quot;store this data but</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L151" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="151"></td>
        <td id="LC151" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  only if no one else has updated since I last fetched it.&quot;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L152" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="152"></td>
        <td id="LC152" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L153" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="153"></td>
        <td id="LC153" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &lt;key&gt; is the key under which the client asks to store the data</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L154" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="154"></td>
        <td id="LC154" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L155" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="155"></td>
        <td id="LC155" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &lt;flags&gt; is an arbitrary 16-bit unsigned integer (written out in</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L156" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="156"></td>
        <td id="LC156" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  decimal) that the server stores along with the data and sends back</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L157" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="157"></td>
        <td id="LC157" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  when the item is retrieved. Clients may use this as a bit field to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L158" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="158"></td>
        <td id="LC158" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  store data-specific information; this field is opaque to the server.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L159" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="159"></td>
        <td id="LC159" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Note that in memcached 1.2.1 and higher, flags may be 32-bits, instead</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L160" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="160"></td>
        <td id="LC160" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  of 16, but you might want to restrict yourself to 16 bits for</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L161" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="161"></td>
        <td id="LC161" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  compatibility with older versions.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L162" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="162"></td>
        <td id="LC162" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L163" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="163"></td>
        <td id="LC163" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &lt;exptime&gt; is expiration time. If it&#39;s 0, the item never expires</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L164" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="164"></td>
        <td id="LC164" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  (although it may be deleted from the cache to make place for other</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L165" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="165"></td>
        <td id="LC165" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  items). If it&#39;s non-zero (either Unix time or offset in seconds from</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L166" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="166"></td>
        <td id="LC166" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  current time), it is guaranteed that clients will not be able to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L167" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="167"></td>
        <td id="LC167" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  retrieve this item after the expiration time arrives (measured by</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L168" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="168"></td>
        <td id="LC168" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  server time). If a negative value is given the item is immediately</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L169" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="169"></td>
        <td id="LC169" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  expired.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L170" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="170"></td>
        <td id="LC170" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L171" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="171"></td>
        <td id="LC171" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &lt;bytes&gt; is the number of bytes in the data block to follow, *not*</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L174" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="174"></td>

</td>
      </tr>

      </tr>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>

</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L243" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="243"></td>
        <td id="LC243" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">If some of the keys appearing in a retrieval request are not sent back</td>

        <td id="L244" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="244"></td>

        <td id="L246" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="246"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L247" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="247"></td>
        <td id="LC247" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">deleted by a client).</td>

        <td id="L274" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="274"></td>
        <td id="LC274" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Increment/Decrement</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L275" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="275"></td>
        <td id="LC275" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">-------------------</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L276" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="276"></td>
        <td id="LC276" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L277" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="277"></td>
        <td id="LC277" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Commands &quot;incr&quot; and &quot;decr&quot; are used to change data for some item</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L278" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="278"></td>
        <td id="LC278" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">in-place, incrementing or decrementing it. The data for the item is</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L279" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="279"></td>
        <td id="LC279" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">treated as decimal representation of a 64-bit unsigned integer.  If</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L280" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="280"></td>
        <td id="LC280" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the current data value does not conform to such a representation, the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L281" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="281"></td>
        <td id="LC281" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">incr/decr commands return an error (memcached &lt;= 1.2.6 treated the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L282" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="282"></td>
        <td id="LC282" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">bogus value as if it were 0, leading to confusion). Also, the item</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L283" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="283"></td>
        <td id="LC283" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">must already exist for incr/decr to work; these commands won&#39;t pretend</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L284" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="284"></td>
        <td id="LC284" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">that a non-existent key exists with value 0; instead, they will fail.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L285" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="285"></td>
        <td id="LC285" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>

</td>

</td>

        <td id="L310" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="310"></td>
        <td id="LC310" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Note that underflow in the &quot;decr&quot; command is caught: if a client tries</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L311" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="311"></td>
        <td id="LC311" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to decrease the value below 0, the new value will be 0.  Overflow in</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC312" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the &quot;incr&quot; command will wrap around the 64 bit mark.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC313" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L314" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="314"></td>
        <td id="LC314" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Note also that decrementing a number such that it loses length isn&#39;t</td>
      </tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L408" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="408"></td>
        <td id="LC408" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">----------</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L409" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="409"></td>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L410" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="410"></td>
        <td id="LC410" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Memcached supports multiple LRU algorithms, with a few tunables. Effort is</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L411" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="411"></td>
        <td id="LC411" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">made to have sane defaults however you are able to tune while the daemon is</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L412" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="412"></td>
        <td id="LC412" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">running.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L413" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="413"></td>
        <td id="LC413" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L414" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="414"></td>
        <td id="LC414" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The traditional model is &quot;flat&quot; mode, which is a single LRU chain per slab</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L415" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="415"></td>
        <td id="LC415" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">class. The newer (with `-o modern` or `-o lru_maintainer`) is segmented into</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L416" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="416"></td>
        <td id="LC416" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">HOT, WARM, COLD. There is also a TEMP LRU. See doc/new_lru.txt for details.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L417" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="417"></td>
        <td id="LC417" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">

        <td id="LC418" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">lru &lt;tune|mode|temp_ttl&gt; &lt;option list&gt;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

</td>

        <td id="LC420" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &quot;tune&quot; takes numeric arguments &quot;percent hot&quot;, &quot;percent warm&quot;,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L421" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="421"></td>
        <td id="LC421" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  &quot;max hot age&quot;, &quot;max warm age factor&quot;. IE: &quot;lru tune 10 25 3600 2.0&quot;.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L422" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="422"></td>
        <td id="LC422" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  This would cap HOT_LRU at 10% of the cache, or tail is idle longer than</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L423" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="423"></td>
        <td id="LC423" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  3600s. WARM_LRU is up to 25% of cache, or tail is idle longer than 2x</td>

        <td id="LC424" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  COLD_LRU.</td>

        <td id="LC426" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &quot;mode&quot; &lt;flat|segmented&gt;: &quot;flat&quot; is traditional mode. &quot;segmented&quot; uses</td>
      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L428" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="428"></td>
        <td id="LC428" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  time. If switching from segmented to flat mode, the background thread will</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L429" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="429"></td>
        <td id="LC429" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  pull items from HOT|WARM into COLD queue.</td>
      </tr>

</td>

        <td id="LC431" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &quot;temp_ttl&quot; &lt;ttl&gt;: If TTL is less than zero, disable usage of TEMP_LRU. If</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L432" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="432"></td>
        <td id="LC432" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  zero or above, items set with a TTL lower than this will go into TEMP_LRU</td>

      </tr>
      <tr>

        <td id="LC434" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  replaced.</td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L546" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="546"></td>
        <td id="LC546" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L547" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="547"></td>
        <td id="LC547" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The response format is in &quot;key=value key2=value2&quot; format, for easy parsing.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L548" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="548"></td>
        <td id="LC548" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Lines are prepending with &quot;ts=&quot; for a timestamp and &quot;gid=&quot; for a global ID</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L549" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="549"></td>
        <td id="LC549" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">number of the log line. Given how logs are collected internally they may be</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L550" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="550"></td>
        <td id="LC550" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">printed out of order. If this is important the GID may be used to put log</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L551" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="551"></td>
        <td id="LC551" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">lines back in order.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L552" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="552"></td>
        <td id="LC552" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L553" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="553"></td>
        <td id="LC553" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The value of keys (and potentially other things) are &quot;URI encoded&quot;. Since most</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L554" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="554"></td>
        <td id="LC554" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">keys used conform to standard ASCII, this should have no effect. For keys with</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L555" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="555"></td>
        <td id="LC555" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">less standard or binary characters, &quot;%NN&quot;&#39;s are inserted to represent the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L556" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="556"></td>
        <td id="LC556" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">byte, ie: &quot;n%2Cfoo&quot; for &quot;n,foo&quot;.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L557" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="557"></td>
        <td id="LC557" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L558" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="558"></td>
        <td id="LC558" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The arguments are:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L559" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="559"></td>
        <td id="LC559" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L560" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="560"></td>
        <td id="LC560" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &quot;fetchers&quot;: Currently emits logs every time an item is fetched internally.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L561" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="561"></td>
        <td id="LC561" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  This means a &quot;set&quot; command would also emit an item_get log, as it checks for</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L562" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="562"></td>
        <td id="LC562" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  an item before replacing it. Multigets should also emit multiple lines.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L563" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="563"></td>
        <td id="LC563" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L564" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="564"></td>
        <td id="LC564" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &quot;mutations&quot;: Currently emits logs when an item is stored in most cases.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L565" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="565"></td>
        <td id="LC565" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Shows errors for most cases when items cannot be stored.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L566" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="566"></td>
        <td id="LC566" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L567" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="567"></td>
        <td id="LC567" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">- &quot;evictions&quot;: Shows some information about items as they are evicted from the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L568" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="568"></td>
        <td id="LC568" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  cache. Useful in seeing if items being evicted were actually used, and which</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L569" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="569"></td>
        <td id="LC569" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  keys are getting removed.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L570" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="570"></td>
        <td id="LC570" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L571" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="571"></td>
        <td id="LC571" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Statistics</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L574" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="574"></td>
        <td id="LC574" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The command &quot;stats&quot; is used to query the server about statistics it</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L575" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="575"></td>
        <td id="LC575" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">maintains and other internal data. It has two forms. Without</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L576" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="576"></td>
        <td id="LC576" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">arguments:</td>

</td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L579" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="579"></td>
        <td id="LC579" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L580" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="580"></td>
        <td id="LC580" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">it causes the server to output general-purpose statistics and</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L581" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="581"></td>
        <td id="LC581" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">settings, documented below.  In the other form it has some arguments:</td>
      </tr>

</td>

      </tr>

</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC585" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Depending on &lt;args&gt;, various internal data is sent by the server. The</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L586" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="586"></td>

        <td id="L591" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="591"></td>
        <td id="LC591" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">General-purpose statistics</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L592" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="592"></td>

        <td id="L594" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="594"></td>
        <td id="LC594" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Upon receiving the &quot;stats&quot; command without arguments, the server sents</td>
      </tr>

</td>

</td>

      </tr>

</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L603" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="603"></td>
        <td id="LC603" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In each line of statistics, &lt;name&gt; is the name of this statistic, and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L604" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="604"></td>
        <td id="LC604" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">&lt;value&gt; is the data.  The following is the list of all names sent in</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC605" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">response to the &quot;stats&quot; command, together with the type of the value</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L606" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="606"></td>
        <td id="LC606" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">sent for this name, and the meaning of the value.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC608" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In the type column below, &quot;32u&quot; means a 32-bit unsigned integer, &quot;64u&quot;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L609" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="609"></td>
        <td id="LC609" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">means a 64-bit unsigned integer. &#39;32u.32u&#39; means two 32-bit unsigned</td>

        <td id="LC878" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The &quot;stats&quot; command with the argument of &quot;sizes&quot; returns information about the</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC879" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">general size and count of all items stored in the cache.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC881" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">lock while it iterates the items. 1.4.27 and greater are safe.</td>
      </tr>

</td>

      <tr>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1093" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1093"></td>
        <td id="LC1093" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1094" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1094"></td>
        <td id="LC1094" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">UDP protocol</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1095" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1095"></td>
        <td id="LC1095" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">------------</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1096" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1096"></td>
        <td id="LC1096" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1097" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1097"></td>
        <td id="LC1097" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For very large installations where the number of clients is high enough</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1098" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1098"></td>
        <td id="LC1098" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">that the number of TCP connections causes scaling difficulties, there is</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1099" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1099"></td>
        <td id="LC1099" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">also a UDP-based interface. The UDP interface does not provide guaranteed</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1100" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1100"></td>
        <td id="LC1100" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">delivery, so should only be used for operations that aren&#39;t required to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1101" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1101"></td>
        <td id="LC1101" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">succeed; typically it is used for &quot;get&quot; requests where a missing or</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1102" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1102"></td>
        <td id="LC1102" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">incomplete response can simply be treated as a cache miss.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1103" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1103"></td>
        <td id="LC1103" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1104" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1104"></td>
        <td id="LC1104" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Each UDP datagram contains a simple frame header, followed by data in the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1105" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1105"></td>
        <td id="LC1105" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">same format as the TCP protocol described above. In the current</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1106" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1106"></td>
        <td id="LC1106" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">implementation, requests must be contained in a single UDP datagram, but</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1107" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1107"></td>
        <td id="LC1107" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">responses may span several datagrams. (The only common requests that would</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1108" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1108"></td>
        <td id="LC1108" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">span multiple datagrams are huge multi-key &quot;get&quot; requests and &quot;set&quot;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1109" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1109"></td>
        <td id="LC1109" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">requests, both of which are more suitable to TCP transport for reliability</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1110" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1110"></td>
        <td id="LC1110" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">reasons anyway.)</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1111" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1111"></td>
        <td id="LC1111" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1112" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1112"></td>
        <td id="LC1112" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The frame header is 8 bytes long, as follows (all values are 16-bit integers</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1113" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1113"></td>
